<span id="line324"></span>        </span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">p</span> <span class="attribute-name">style</span>="<a class="attribute-value">font-size: 3em; font-weight: bold; text-align: center; margin-top: .5em;</a>"&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line325"></span>  Together, by moving bytes and bananas, Maersk developers power globally integrated trade.
<span id="line326"></span></span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">p</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line327"></span>
<span id="line328"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">p</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line329"></span>Welcome to the Maersk developer community. Below you will find all of the documentation to guide you through a successful integration with our APIs.
<span id="line330"></span></span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">p</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line331"></span>
<span id="line332"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">p</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line333"></span>For API keys, troubleshooting or just a general chat. Please get in touch with the Maersk API team at </span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">a</span> <span class="attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="attribute-value" href="mailto:api@maersk.com">mailto:api@maersk.com</a>"&gt;</span><span>api@maersk.com</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">a</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line334"></span></span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">p</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line335"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">h1</span> <span class="attribute-name">id</span>='<a class="attribute-value">backwards-compatibility-amp-versioning</a>'&gt;</span><span>Backwards Compatibility <span class="entity"><span>&amp;</span>amp;</span> Versioning</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">h1</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line336"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">p</span>&gt;</span><span>We will do everything we can to maintain backwards compatibility as we bring you new features. However, we won<span class="entity"><span>&amp;</span>#39;</span>t always get it right first time. When we don<span class="entity"><span>&amp;</span>#39;</span>t, we need to provide you with an updated API without disrupting your current integration. To this end we have defined a few transparent rules around backwards compatibility and versioning to make your life easier and more predictable. To avoid integration troubles, make sure you are developing robust code by expecting the API to flex with new parameters, elements etc. We have detailed the expected changes below, so you can understand how our APIs will change over time.</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">p</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line337"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">h2</span> <span class="attribute-name">id</span>='<a class="attribute-value">we-will-be-routinely-without-a-new-version</a>'&gt;</span><span>We will be routinely (without a new version)</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">h2</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line338"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">ul</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line339"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>Adding new parameters to requests (query, path and header)</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line340"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>Adding new elements into the response payload</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line341"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>Re-ordering elements in the response payload (no hierarchy modification though)</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line342"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>That gets you the new features you need from each API and you can consume them whenever you want</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line343"></span></span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">ul</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line344"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">h2</span> <span class="attribute-name">id</span>='<a class="attribute-value">we-will-release-a-new-version-when-we</a>'&gt;</span><span>We will release a new version when we</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">h2</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line345"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">ul</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line346"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>Remove or modify existing request parameters (query, path and header) including making any mandatory parameters optional</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line347"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>Remove or modify existing response payload including key names and data types</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line348"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>Completely refactor an API</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">li</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line349"></span></span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">ul</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line350"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">h2</span> <span class="attribute-name">id</span>='<a class="attribute-value">when-do-we-deprecate-apis</a>'&gt;</span><span>When do we deprecate APIs?</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">h2</span>&gt;</span><span>
<span id="line351"></span></span><span>&lt;<span class="start-tag">p</span>&gt;</span><span>When we decide to release a new version of an API we will keep the previous version available for 3 months. You will be notified about this and will be expected to make the necessary changes with your integration to avoid a disruption of service in your application.</span><span>&lt;/<span class="end-tag">p</span>&gt;</span><span>
